<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ะฒะพะปะบะพะดะฐะฒ.html>ะฒะพะปะบะพะดะฐฬะฒ</a></strong> โข (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">volkodรกv</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ะฒะพะปะบะพะดะฐะฒ.html>ะฒะพะปะบะพะดะฐฬะฒะฐ</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ะฒะพะปะบะพะดะฐะฒ.html>ะฒะพะปะบะพะดะฐฬะฒั</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ะฒะพะปะบะพะดะฐะฒ.html>ะฒะพะปะบะพะดะฐฬะฒะพะฒ</a></b>)

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*vัlna</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">โ</span><span class="mention-gloss">wool</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">โ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*hโwฤบฬฅhโnehโ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">โ</span><span class="mention-gloss">wool</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">โ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ะฒะพะปะฝะพะฒะฐัั.html>ะฒะพะปะฝะพะฒะฐฬัั</a></strong> โข (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">volnovรกtสน</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ะฒะทะฒะพะปะฝะพะฒะฐัั.html>ะฒะทะฒะพะปะฝะพะฒะฐฬัั</a></b>)

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ะฒะพะปะพะบะฝะพ.html>ะฒะพะปะพะบะฝะพฬ</a></strong> โข (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">voloknรณ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ะฒะพะปะพะบะฝะพ.html>ะฒะพะปะพะบะฝะฐฬ</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ะฒะพะปะพะบะฝะพ.html>ะฒะพะปะพฬะบะฝะฐ</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ะฒะพะปะพะบะฝะพ.html>ะฒะพะปะพฬะบะพะฝ</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">ะฒะพะปะพะบะพฬะฝัะต</b>)

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*volsั</i>. Doublet of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">ะฒะปะฐั</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vlas</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, a borrowing from Old Church Slavonic. From <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*wel-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">โ</span><span class="mention-gloss">hair; wool</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">โ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p><p>Cognates with ๏ฟผ๏ฟผ๏ฟผ๏ฟผ๏ฟผ๏ฟผ๏ฟผOld Persian๏ฟผ๏ฟผ (vars), Persian ฺฏุฑุณโ (gurs, โcurled hairโ), Kurdish <i>pirรง</i> (โhairโ) and Lithuanian <i>๏ฟผ๏ฟผvalaฤฉ๏ฟผ๏ฟผ,</i> Sanskrit๏ฟผ๏ฟผ๏ฟผ๏ฟผ๏ฟผ๏ฟผ๏ฟผ๏ฟผ เคตเคฒเฅเคถ (vรกlลa, โtwig, sprout). Akin to Old Armenian ีพีกึีฝ (vars), an Iranian borrowing.
</p>

</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:ัััะตััะฒะธัะตะปัะฝะพะต.html>ะกััะตััะฒะธฬัะตะปัะฝะพะต</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:ะฝะตะพะดััะตะฒะปะตะฝะฝัะน.html>ะฝะตะพะดััะตะฒะปัะฝะฝะพะต</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:ะผัะถัะบะพะน.html>ะผัะถัะบะพฬะน</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ัะพะด.html>ัะพะด</a>, 2-ะต <a href = vnd.unilang:ัะบะปะพะฝะตะฝะธะต.html>ัะบะปะพะฝะตฬะฝะธะต</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:ัะธะฟ.html>ัะธะฟ</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ัะบะปะพะฝะตะฝะธะต.html>ัะบะปะพะฝะตฬะฝะธั</a> 3*b  <a href = vnd.unilang:ะฟะพ.html>ะฟะพ</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ะบะปะฐััะธัะธะบะฐัะธั.html>ะบะปะฐััะธัะธะบะฐฬัะธะธ</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ะฐ.html>ะ</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:ะฐ.html>ะ</a>. ะะฐะปะธะทะฝัะบะฐ).
